{ED:3._ROBERT_CELY_AT_LONDON_TO_GEORGE_CELY,_13_APRIL_1476}

AUTHOR:ROBERT_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
LETTER:CELY_002:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
A=o= lxxvj CELY,4.002.20

AUTHOR:ROBERT_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
LETTER:CELY_002:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Welbelouyd brother , I recomaund me herttely to yow , fferthermore
informynge yow that the xiij day of Aprell the +geere aboue sayd , I
Robard Cely haue ressayuyd off Wylliam Eston , mersar of London , xij
li. ster. to pay at Andewarpe in Sencyon martte the xxiiij day of June
, for euery nobyll of vj s. viij d. ster. , vij s x d. Fllemeche ,
CELY,4.002.21

AUTHOR:ROBERT_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
LETTER:CELY_002:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
and I pray yow to delyuer to the sayd Wylliam Eston xij li. starlynge
at the same ratte , takynge a byll of ys honde to paye at London the
sayd xij li. at a day as longe hafter +te day as I toke the mony wp
beffore . CELY,4.002.22

AUTHOR:ROBERT_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
LETTER:CELY_002:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
In wettnes herof I sette my seell at London the xiij day of Aprell .
CELY,4.002.23

AUTHOR:ROBERT_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_
LETTER:CELY_002:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
per Robard Cely . CELY,4.002.24

AUTHOR:ROBERT_CELY:MALE:BROTHER:_:_

RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:CELY_004:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Ryght reuerent syre and my specyall frend , I recomaund me vnto you .
CELY,5.004.54

AUTHOR:WILLIAM_MARYON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:CELY_004:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Ferdermor , and yt plesse you , ye schall vnderstond that Y haue
schypped in the George of London , Wylliam Wellson beyng master , ix
packys d. of fellys contaynyng iij M=l= viij=c=l fellys , the whych
fellys leyyt in the for-rom of the sayd schyppe , v packys iij=c= d. ,
and the remenant leyyt abaft the mast vpon John Tamys <P_6> fellys ,
the wyche fellys war Thomas Kestenys , CELY,6.004.55

AUTHOR:WILLIAM_MARYON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:CELY_004:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
and thay war arested be Thomas Hadam for the som of lx li .
CELY,6.004.56

AUTHOR:WILLIAM_MARYON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:CELY_004:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Syr , ye schall vnderstond that Thomas Kesten hat y-wreten vnto me that
Y schuld fynd the way and the men to saff the cortte harmeles her , and
taake the fellys for myn own , that Y schuld be sewyr of that som in
dyschargyng of the sewyrteys and allso in party of payment of seche
goodys as he ys owyng vnto me , as ye know well , CELY,6.004.57

AUTHOR:WILLIAM_MARYON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:CELY_004:M4:1476:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
and therfor , syr , I pray you that ye woll ressayue them as myn own
proper good , CELY,6.004.58

euery vj s. viij d. ster. and iiij monthes day after the resayuyng in
the marte , for the weche C li. ster. ye schall haue a letter of
payment of John Hossyer to be payd to me at London in Octobor next com
, CELY,49.043.897

LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
I grete you wyll , CELY,76.061.1311

AUTHOR:RICHARD_CELY_SR:MALE:FATHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:SON:_:_
LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
and I haue resayuyd a letter from you wryte at Caleys the xiij day of
May , the weche letter I haue wyll understande , of youre beyng at the
martys , and of the sale of my medell woll desyred be John Descermer
and John Underhay , werefor be the grace of God I am avysyd for to
schepe thys forsayd xxix sarplerys , the weche I bogwyt of Wyll
Medewynter of Norlayche xxvj sarplerys , the weche ys fayre woll , as
the woll packar Wyll <P_77> Breten saythe to me . CELY,77.061.1312

AUTHOR:RICHARD_CELY_SR:MALE:FATHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:SON:_:_
LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
And also the iij sarplerys of the Recturs ys fayre woll - meche fynar
woll nor was the +gere before , the weche I schepede afore Ester laste
paste . CELY,77.061.1313

AUTHOR:RICHARD_CELY_SR:MALE:FATHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:SON:_:_
LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR

LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
but I haue non schepyde as yete , CELY,77.061.1315

RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:SON:_:_
LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
but I wyll after thys halydayys , for the weche I wyll ye orden for the
frayth and hoder costys . CELY,77.061.1316

AUTHOR:RICHARD_CELY_SR:MALE:FATHER:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:SON:_:_
LETTER:CELY_061:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Thys same day youre broder Rychard Cely ys rede to Norlay for to se and
caste a sorte of fell for me and anoder sorte of fell for you and
Rychard Cely . CELY,77.061.1317

Right wursull and welbelouyd cosyn , Y recomavnde me vnto wyth all myne
harte , desiring to here off youre gode hele and welfare , the wiche
allmyghty Jhesu mayntene and encrece euer to his plesur and to youre
hartis desire . CELY,77.062.1335

AUTHOR:JOHN_CELY:MALE:COUSIN:_:_
RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:COUSIN:_:_
LETTER:CELY_062:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
Firthermore Cosen , and hit plese you to vnderstand , ther wasse in
tyme paste a verians and a jarre betwyne Richard Bowell and my maystur
youre fadur for a dute that he schulde owe to my said maystur youre
fadur , CELY,77.062.1336

RECIPIENT:GEORGE_CELY:MALE:COUSIN:_:_

fadur acordyd and agreid for that mater , CELY,77.062.1337

the dede of whyntter , and let ren the next somar , and then he schawll
be sawhe whell he ys hors . CELY,177.132.2890

abyll to contente you , nor non oder ; the wiche I wolde be $lothe to
do , bothe for myn owne pore name and for my cheldrenys , as Jhesu
deffende . CELY,218.140.3098

but as yett they be nott agreed amongyst hemselffe . Wherffor they hawe
sent ynto Braband and ynto Holond and Zelond that eueryche of thes
contreys doo send to Brugys serten wysemen wyth ffull auctoryte of ther
contrey ffor to coomen and talke wyth the <P_244> Gauntenersse and them
, and that maye take syche wayes and concluson amongyst them as they
can dryve be reson moste benyffycyall for them and ther contreys .
CELY,244.147.3239
